NEPAnode 1 (GeoNode 2.0) to NEPAnode 2 (GeoNode 2.4) Data Migration Notes
by Don Bales on 2015-03-03

So let's try again!

service apache2 start
service postgresql start
service tomcat7 start
rm -R /usr/share/geoserver
rm -R /var/www/geonode
apt-get purge -y geonode
apt-get purge -y geoserver-geonode
service apache2 stop
apt-get purge -y apache2
service postgresql stop
apt-get purge -y postgresql-9.3
apt-get purge -y postgis
service tomcat7 start
rm -R /etc/tomcat7/Catalina/localhost
apt-get purge -y tomcat7
apt-get autoremove -y


And now install:

apt-get install -y geonode

#
# GeoNode specific settings
#
SITEURL = "http://54.236.235.110/"

#The site name, used throughout templates:
SITE_NAME = 'NEPAnode'

# Uncomment the following to receive emails whenever there are errors in GeoNode
ADMINS = (
            ('John Jediny', 'nepanode@gmail.com'),
         )

# Uncomment the following to use a Gmail account as the email backend
EMAIL_USE_TLS = True
EMAIL_HOST = 'smtp.gmail.com'
EMAIL_HOST_USER = 'nepanode@gmail.com'
EMAIL_HOST_PASSWORD = <only john knows>
EMAIL_PORT = 587

# A tuple of hosts the proxy can send requests to.
PROXY_ALLOWED_HOSTS = ()



I modified /etc/geonode/local_settings.py as follows:

# SITENAME and SITEURL modified by Don Bales on 2015-03-03 17:57
SITENAME = 'NEPAnode'
SITEURL = 'http://54.197.226.56/'

# ALLOWED_HOSTS added by Don Bales on 2015-03-03 17:57
ALLOWED_HOSTS = [ u'54.197.226.56', u'localhost', u'127.0.0.1', ]

# ADMINS added by Don Bales on 2015-03-03 17:59
ADMINS = (
            ('John Jediny', 'nepanode@gmail.com'),
            ('Don Bales', 'dbales@anl.gov'),
         )

# EMAIL... added by Don Bales on 2015-03-03 17:59
EMAIL_USE_TLS = True
EMAIL_HOST = 'smtp.gmail.com'
EMAIL_HOST_USER = 'nepanode@gmail.com'
EMAIL_HOST_PASSWORD = <only john knows>
EMAIL_PORT = 587

Create a .pgpass file in /root

root@ip-172-31-9-248:~$ nano .pgpass

hostname:port:database:username:password
localhost:5432:geonode:*:<set by install>

root@ip-172-31-9-248:~$ chmod 600 .pgpass

psql -h localhost geonode geonode


backup of the initial database:
*******************************

root@ip-172-31-23-51:~# sudo -u postgres -i
postgres@ip-172-31-23-51:~$ pwd
/var/lib/postgresql

pg_dumpall -g -f geonode_2.4_globals_initial.sql

pg_dumpall    -f geonode_2.4_full_initial.sql

pg_dump       -f geonode_2.4_database_geonode_initial.sql geonode

pg_dump       -f geonode_2.4_database_geonode_data_initial.sql geonode_data

Shut down apache2 and geoserver (tomcat7) and before migrating:
service apache2 stop
service tomcat7 stop
service --status-all

Yes, they are down and postgres is up and running.


Now restore the PostGIS database, geonode2_upload, from NEPAnode 1
to NEPAnode 2's PostGIS database, geonode_data:

Since NEPAnode 1 used PostGIS 2.0 and NEPAnode 2 uses PostGIS 2.1,
we need to restore the schema objects first, then the data second.
When restoring the schema objects, pg_restore will generate errors
for every PostGIS 2.0 object that also exists as a PostGIS 2.1
object.  That's OK, and expected.  But it will successfully create
any upload tables, etc.

schema first...

sudo -u postgres -i

pg_restore -s --clean -d geonode_data /home/ubuntu/nepanode1_geonode2_upload_2015-02-27.pgr > pg_restore_nepanode1_geonode2_upload_schema_only.txt 2>&1

OK.

data second...

pg_restore -a --clean -d geonode_data /home/ubuntu/nepanode1_geonode2_upload_2015-02-27.pgr > pg_restore_nepanode1_geonode2_upload_data_only.txt 2>&1

Now clean up the owenrship and privileges

find /var/lib/geoserver_data -name "*" -exec chown tomcat7 {} \;

find /var/lib/geoserver_data -name "*" -exec chgrp tomcat7 {} \;

find /var/lib/geoserver_data -name "*" -type d -exec chmod 775 {} \;

find /var/lib/geoserver_data -name "*" -type f -exec chmod 664 {} \;


Modify the web.xml file for geoserver to point to /var/lib/geoserver

root@ip-172-31-23-51:~# find / -name "web.xml" | grep geoserver
/usr/share/geoserver/WEB-INF/web.xml

root@ip-172-31-23-51:~# nano /usr/share/geoserver/WEB-INF/web.xml

    <context-param>
        <param-name>GEOSERVER_DATA_DIR</param-name>
        <param-value>/var/lib/geoserver_data</param-value>
    </context-param>

At this point, I should be able to start Geoserver.  Should I try?


GEONODE DATA MIGRATION
======================

First step? Open up the port in order to connect remotely:

nano /etc/postgresql/9.3/main/pg_hba.conf

root@ip-172-31-23-51:~# nano /etc/postgresql/9.3/main/pg_hba.conf

# TYPE  DATABASE        USER            ADDRESS                 METHOD
host    all             all             146.137.33.66/32        password


nano /etc/postgresql/9.3/main/postgresql.conf

root@ip-172-31-23-51:~# nano /etc/postgresql/9.3/main/postgresql.conf


listen_addresses = '*'
log_connections = on


service postgresql restart


Execute migration scripts.

Done.

Execute set sequence values.

psql -h 54.197.226.56 -qtA geonode geonode < create_nepanode_2_set_sequence_values.sql > nepanode_2_set_sequence_values.sql

psql -h 54.197.226.56 -qtA geonode geonode < nepanode_2_set_sequence_values.sql > nepanode_2_set_sequence_values.txt

Done.

The moment of truth.  Will the application run now?


No.

LAYERS_LAYER PROBLEMS
=====================

update layers_layer
set    store = 'datastore'
where  store = 'geonode2_upload';

update layers_layer
set    charset = 'UTF-8'
where  charset = 'UTF8';

update base_resourcebase
set    detail_url = (select '/layers/'||replace(layers_layer.typename, ':', '%3A') from layers_layer where layers_layer.resourcebase_ptr_id = base_resourcebase.id)
where  id in (select layers_layer.resourcebase_ptr_id from layers_layer where detail_url is NULL);

update base_resourcebase
set    polymorphic_ctype_id = 41
where  id in (select resourcebase_ptr_id from layers_layer)
and    polymorphic_ctype_id is NULL;




MAPS_MAP PROBLEMS
=================

update base_resourcebase
set    detail_url = '/maps/'||id
where  id in (select maps_map.resourcebase_ptr_id from maps_map)
and    detail_url is NULL;

update base_resourcebase
set    polymorphic_ctype_id = 45
where  id in (select resourcebase_ptr_id from maps_map)
and    polymorphic_ctype_id is NULL;



DOCUMENTS_DOCUMENT PROBLEMS
===========================

update base_resourcebase
set    polymorphic_ctype_id = 48
where  id in (select resourcebase_ptr_id from documents_document)
and    polymorphic_ctype_id is NULL;
